1574162696--SELECT a.bat_no,a.system_id,a.create_time,a.status,c.cbat,c.check_stock,SUM(b.payment) as payment,b.payment_time,c.total_fee,c.take_fee,c.take_tid_fee,c.system_name,d.pay_type FROM u13123456789_sync_tid_bat AS a
			LEFT JOIN (SELECT bat_no,payment,payment_time FROM u13123456789_sync_tid_pay_log) AS b ON a.bat_no=b.bat_no
			left join (
				select a.bat_no,count(1) as cbat,check_stock,print_type,close_unique_code,sum(b.now_price) as total_fee,sum(if(a.is_take=1,a.take_price,0)) as take_fee,sum(if(a.is_take=1,a.price,0)) as take_tid_fee,c.system_name,b.prd_no from u13123456789_sync_tid_items  a 
				left join (SELECT prd_no,now_price FROM u13123456789_producte_take_items a
left JOIN (SELECT MAX(id) AS id FROM u13123456789_producte_take_items GROUP BY prd_no) AS b ON b.id=a.id) as b on b.prd_no=a.prd_no
				left join (select system_id,cus_name as system_name from u13123456789_cust) as c on a.system_id=c.system_id 
				group by a.bat_no
			) as c on c.bat_no=a.bat_no
			left join (select system_id,payment_type as pay_type from u13123456789_cust) as d on d.system_id=a.system_id
			WHERE 1=1 and a.status = 0 and a.bat_no like '%2%' GROUP BY a.bat_no,a.system_id,a.create_time,a.status
			UNION ALL
			SELECT a.bat_no,a.system_id,a.create_time,a.status,c.cbat,c.check_stock,SUM(b.payment) as payment,b.payment_time,c.total_fee,c.take_fee,c.take_tid_fee,c.system_name,d.pay_type FROM u13123456789_sync_tid_bat AS a
			LEFT JOIN (SELECT bat_no,payment,payment_time FROM u13123456789_sync_tid_pay_log) AS b ON a.bat_no=b.bat_no
			left join (
				select a.bat_no,count(1) as cbat,check_stock,print_type,close_unique_code,sum(b.now_price) as total_fee,sum(if(a.is_take=1,a.take_price,0)) as take_fee,sum(if(a.is_take=1,a.price,0)) as take_tid_fee,c.system_name,b.prd_no from u13123456789_sync_tid_items  a 
				left join (SELECT prd_no,now_price FROM u13123456789_producte_take_items a
left JOIN (SELECT MAX(id) AS id FROM u13123456789_producte_take_items GROUP BY prd_no) AS b ON b.id=a.id) as b on b.prd_no=a.prd_no
				left join (select system_id,cus_name as system_name from u13123456789_cust) as c on a.system_id=c.system_id 
				group by a.bat_no
			) as c on c.bat_no=a.bat_no
			left join (select system_id,payment_type as pay_type from u13123456789_cust) as d on d.system_id=a.system_id
			WHERE 1=1 and a.status = 0 and c.prd_no  like '%2%' GROUP BY a.bat_no,a.system_id,a.create_time,a.status limit 0,5

				left join (SELECT prd_no,now_price FROM u13123456789_producte_take_items a
left JOIN (SELECT MAX(id) AS id FROM u13123456789_producte_take_items GROUP BY prd_no) AS b ON b.id=a.id) as b on b.prd_no=a.prd_no
				left join (select system_id,cus_name as system_name from u13123456789_cust) as c on a.system_id=c.system_id WHERE a.check_stock=1
				group by a.bat_no
			) as c on c.bat_no=a.bat_no
			left join (select system_id,payment_type as pay_type from u13123456789_cust) as d on d.system_id=a.system_id
			WHERE 1=1 and a.status = 3 and c.close_unique_code = 0   and a.bat_no like '%2%' GROUP BY a.bat_no,a.system_id,a.create_time,a.status
			UNION ALL
			SELECT a.bat_no,a.system_id,a.create_time,a.status,c.cbat,c.check_stock,SUM(b.payment) as payment,b.payment_time,c.total_fee,c.take_fee,c.take_tid_fee,c.system_name,d.pay_type FROM u13123456789_sync_tid_bat AS a
			LEFT JOIN (SELECT bat_no,payment,payment_time FROM u13123456789_sync_tid_pay_log) AS b ON a.bat_no=b.bat_no
			left join (
				select a.bat_no,count(1) as cbat,check_stock,print_type,close_unique_code,sum(b.now_price) as total_fee,sum(if(a.is_take=1,a.take_price,0)) as take_fee,sum(if(a.is_take=1,a.price,0)) as take_tid_fee,c.system_name,b.prd_no from u13123456789_sync_tid_items  a 
				left join (SELECT prd_no,now_price FROM u13123456789_producte_take_items a
left JOIN (SELECT MAX(id) AS id FROM u13123456789_producte_take_items GROUP BY prd_no) AS b ON b.id=a.id) as b on b.prd_no=a.prd_no
				left join (select system_id,cus_name as system_name from u13123456789_cust) as c on a.system_id=c.system_id WHERE a.check_stock=1
				group by a.bat_no
			) as c on c.bat_no=a.bat_no
			left join (select system_id,payment_type as pay_type from u13123456789_cust) as d on d.system_id=a.system_id
			WHERE 1=1 and a.status = 3 and c.close_unique_code = 0   and c.prd_no  like '%2%' GROUP BY a.bat_no,a.system_id,a.create_time,a.status limit 0,5
